id=\"front-content-two\" class=\"front-content widget-area\">\n\t<aside id=\"text-22\" class=\"widget widget_text\">\t\t\t<div class=\"textwidget\"><h3> your feedback...</h3>\n\n<blockquote class=\"comment\"> \nWe fattened feeder pigs into market hogs on the farm. When the pigs were weaned, we had to make noise and call for them when feeding time rolled around so they’d know it was time to get fed.\n\nIt didn’t take long before they associated the sound of the metal bucket scooping up corn with feeding time, and we no longer had to call the pigs, they came running, mouths open and hungry for slop.\n\nThat’s what I see when turning on CNN or FOX or MSNBC, etc. People are so well-programmed, that when they turn the Boob Tube to those channels, they sit on the couch, mouth wide open, expecting news, but all they get is slop..<cite> Greg Bacon  on  <a href=\"https://off-guardian.org/2017/03/15/letters-to-editor-of-europhysics-news-follow-up-to-jones-et-al/#comment-60389\">”is Europhysics News announcing it will censor science papers on political grounds?\" </a></cite>\n</blockquote>\n\n<blockquote class=\"comment\">When wealth and the power it brings to bear can influence the viability of a scientists future it also leads to the inescapable logic that in too many cases, the scientist who toes the political and scientific “line” of concordance will ultimately be awarded a future while those who question or offer science in contradiction can be silenced. This is a worrying development in the war on information\n<cite>Mohandeer  on <a href=\"https://off-guardian.org/2017/03/15/letters-to-editor-of-europhysics-news-follow-up-to-jones-et-al/comment-page-1/#comment-60323\">is Europhysics News announcing it will censor science papers on political grounds?\" </a></cite>\n</blockquote></div>\n\t\t</aside></div><!-- #front-content-two --><div id=\"front-sidebar-two\" class=\"front-sidebar widget-area\" rel=\"author\">Admin</a>\t\t\t\t</div><!-- end .entry-author -->\n\t\t\t\t<p class=\"summary\">Chemical weapons are an invention of the western war machine. Introduced into trench warfare by the French in 1915, over 190,000 tons of chemical weapons were produced during World War 1. There were an estimated 1.3 million casualties caused by chemicals during the war, with 90,000 fatalities</p>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-date\"><a
